    "one of the original motivations for categorifying quantum groups was to provide a representation theoretic explanation for the existence of khovanov homology and other link homologies categorifying quantum link invariants . just as the jones polynomial is described representation theoretically by the quantum group @xmath5 and tensor powers of its two dimensional representation",
    ", the categorification of the jones polynomial via khovanov homology should be described in terms of the 2-representation theory of the categorified quantum group associated to @xmath5 .",
    "currently , the link between categorified quantum groups and khovanov homology follows the indirect path through webster s work on categorified tensor products  @xcite .",
    "this connection utilizes an isomorphism relating webster s categorifications of tensor products with categories associated to blocks of parabolic graded category @xmath6 .",
    "categorifications associated with category @xmath6 were initiated by bernstein , frenkel , and khovanov  @xcite and were further developed in @xcite .",
    "the relation to the familiar picture - world  @xcite of khovanov homology then relies on several technical results of stroppel  @xcite relating the knot homologies constructed using category @xmath6 to khovanov s more elementary construction  @xcite .",
    "more generally , for link homology theories associated with fundamental @xmath7 representations , webster describes an isomorphism relating his construction to sussan s category @xmath6 based link homology theory  @xcite , which is related via koszul duality to a theory defined by mazorchuk and stroppel  @xcite . when @xmath8 , the latter of these link homologies can then be identified  @xcite with khovanov s more elementary construction  @xcite of @xmath3 link homology defined using singular cobordisms called foams .",
    "alternatively , there is an algebro - geometric construction of khovanov homology and related @xmath7 link homologies due to cautis and kamnitzer  @xcite .",
    "these knot homologies arise from derived categories of coherent sheaves on algebraic varieties associated to orbits in the affine grassmannian . in the @xmath4 case",
    "this knot homology agrees with khovanov homology  ( * ? ? ?",
    "* theorem 8.2 ) and these geometric categories can be understood as 2-representations of categorified quantum groups  @xcite .",
    "these link homologies are related to those of seidel - smith  @xcite and manolescu  @xcite by mirror symmetry .    in this article",
    ", we provide a direct construction of foam based @xmath7 link homology theories for @xmath9 or @xmath8 intrinsically in terms of categorified quantum groups .",
    "we show that all of the components involved in these knot homologies are already present within the structure of categorified quantum groups including the relations in foam categories and the complexes defining the braiding . utilizing cautis - rozansky categorified clasps  @xcite we also obtain categorified projectors lifting jones - wenzl idempotents and their @xmath3 analogs purely from the higher relations of categorified quantum groups . in the @xmath4 case",
    "this work reveals the importance of a modified class of foams introduced by christian blanchet  @xcite , suggesting that this version of the foam category is most natural from the perspective of categorified quantum groups . in the @xmath3 case",
    "these results suggest a similar modified version of the @xmath3 foam category",
    ".      recall that in categorified representation theory , @xmath10-vector spaces @xmath11 with decompositions into weight spaces @xmath12 , are replaced by graded categories @xmath13 , and instead of linear maps between spaces , chevalley generators act by functors @xmath14 , @xmath15 satisfying quantum serre relations up to isomorphism of functors . the higher structure of categorified representation theory appears at the level of natural transformations between these functors . in most instances when @xmath16 admits a categorical action of this form , the natural transformations that appear between functors are predictable and can be systematically described .",
    "a key part of this structure is that @xmath17 is a left and right adjoint for @xmath18 and that the endomorphisms of @xmath19 are acted upon by the so called klr algebras developed in  @xcite .    in @xcite",
    "it was suggested that the full structure of categorical representations of @xmath20 is described by a 2-functor from an additive 2-category @xmath21 .",
    "this 2-category categorifies lusztig s modified version @xmath22  @xcite of the quantum group @xmath20 .",
    "the objects of @xmath23 are indexed by the weight lattice of @xmath24 , 1-morphisms correspond to the elements of @xmath22 , and the 2-morphisms govern the natural transformations that appear in categorical representations",
    ". however , the 2-category @xmath23 has additional relations on 2-morphisms beyond specified adjoints and klr relations .",
    "we refer to the collection of relations on 2-morphisms as  higher relations \" because they can be viewed as replacements for the quantum serre relations .",
    "indeed , these higher relations give rise to explicit isomorphisms lifting the defining relations in @xmath22 , while simultaneously controlling the grothendieck group of @xmath21 , allowing for a @xmath25$]-algebra isomorphism between its split grothendieck ring @xmath26 and the integral version of @xmath22 . under this isomorphism , the images of indecomposable 1-morphisms from @xmath23 map to the canonical basis of @xmath22  @xcite .    here",
    "we show that these higher relations also encode the information needed to construct _ all _ @xmath4 and @xmath3 knot homology theories in a framework where computations are accessible .",
    "the key insight for our elementary construction of knot homologies from categorified quantum groups is the fundamental observation of cautis , kamnitzer and licata that the @xmath27-matrix describing the braiding in an @xmath28-fold tensor product of fundamental representations of @xmath16 in reshetikhin - turaev link invariants can be obtained from a deformed weyl group action associated with @xmath29  @xcite .",

    "the observations from the previous section suggest an approach to obtaining diagrammatic @xmath133 link homologies using categorical skew howe duality . in his work categorifying the @xmath3 polynomial , khovanov utilized certain singular web cobordisms called foams  @xcite . in @xcite",
    "these singular surfaces were generalized to the @xmath7 case to supply a diagrammatic counterpart of khovanov - rozansky homology  @xcite .",
    "these foams also appear to be connected with category @xmath139  @xcite and with soergel bimodules  @xcite .",
    "however , unlike khovanov s construction for @xmath3 , there is no known finite set of relations on @xmath7 foams for @xmath140 that guarantee any closed foam can be evaluated to an element of the ground ring . for general @xmath7 ,",
    "matrix factorizations become the primary computation tool  @xcite , and the only way to evaluate a closed foam is through the mysterious kapustin - li formula  @xcite . for foams",
    "this formula was discovered by khovanov and rozansky  @xcite generalizing work of the physicists vafa  @xcite , kapustin , and li  @xcite .",
    "it arises from the topological landau - ginzburg model associated to components of the foam .",
    "a purely combinatorial foam construction of @xmath7 link homology remains an important open problem .",
    "foams can be viewed as a categorification of webs .",
    "indeed , this point of view motivates our approach to constructing @xmath7 link homologies for @xmath9 and @xmath8 . in section  [ sec : foams ] we describe 2-categories of @xmath28-sheeted @xmath133 foams categorifying the above web categories .",
    "we define 2-functors @xmath141 for @xmath9 and @xmath8 .",
    "the existence of such functors was predicted by khovanov and previously defined by mackaay in the @xmath8 case working in the restrictive setting of @xmath142 coefficients in @xcite where he called them `` foamation '' 2-functors .",
    "here we reinterpret mackaay s work ( and extend it to the @xmath4 case ) using skew howe duality , defining foamation functors for @xmath143 with integer coefficients . working over @xmath144 ,",
    "it is not obvious for @xmath9 how to connect categorified quantum groups with the bar - natan s foam description of khovanov homology .",

    "however , the signs under this assignment do not match .",
    "one can try to rescale the foamation functors , but one quickly finds that there is no way to fix the signs under this assignment .    the difficulty in matching the neck - cutting relation with the nilhecke relation is closely related to the solution of another famous problem related to khovanov homology . as originally defined ,",
    "khovanov homology is a projective functorial invariant , meaning that to a cobordism @xmath148 between two tangles one can assign a map @xmath149 between the respective homologies well defined only up to a @xmath150 sign  @xcite .",
    "clark , morrison and walker  @xcite , and independently caprau  @xcite , showed that the functoriality of khovanov homology could be fixed by considering modified foam categories . from the representation - theoretic point of view , these foam categories keep track of the fact that the defining representation of @xmath5 is non - canonically isomorphic to its dual .",
    "keeping track of this information gives rise to a fully functorial tangle invariant .",
    "for both of these fixes to khovanov homology one must work with foams defined over the gaussian integers @xmath151 $ ] .",
    "christian blanchet proposed yet another construction fixing the functoriality of khovanov homology  @xcite .",
    "he works with an enhanced version of the foam category where one labels facets by elements of the set @xmath152 .",
    "the 2-labeled facets are the primary difference from the previous two constructions .",
    "the presence of these 2-labeled facets introduces additional signs that are not present in the cmw or caprau approaches to functoriality .",
    "blanchet s approach gives rise to a functorial version of khovanov homology defined over the integers  @xcite .",
    "these modified foam categories are quite natural from the representation theoretic viewpoint . in the skew howe framework",
    ", foams naturally provide a representation of @xmath153 . seen from this perspective , the foams introduced by blanchet keep track of the difference between the trivial representation @xmath154 and the determinant representation @xmath155 . as @xmath5 representations",
    "there is of course no difference between these two representations , but it appears that blanchet s approach has additional information that contributes additional signs coming from the 2-labeled facets corresponding to the determinant representation @xmath155 .    in this article , we construct foamation functors into both the cmw foam categories as well as the foam categories of blanchet . to define the functors into the cmw foam categories one must continue working with complex coefficients , while blanchet s foam categories naturally admit foamation functors defined over the integers .",
    "this suggests that blanchet s approach is the most natural from the perspective of categorified representation theory .",
    "it is also interesting to note that the @xmath4 knot homology most closely related to categorified quantum groups is integral and functorial .",
    "it turns out that in the @xmath8 case it is possible to modify mackaay s definition of the foamation functors to work over @xmath144 , although this requires rather complicated and unnatural sign assignments .",
    "motivated by the @xmath4 case , we consider a modified @xmath3 foam category that incorporates additional 3-labeled facets . to distinguish these foams from the usual @xmath3 foams we call them blanchet @xmath3 foams .",
    "we show that there are 2-functors into blanchet @xmath3 foams with much more natural sign assignments for the generating 2-morphisms in @xmath156 .",
    "there is also a natural construction of a forgetful 2-functor into the usual @xmath3 foams defined intrinsically in terms of the topology of the blanchet foams . taking the composite of these 2-functors provides an explanation for the complicated signs occurring in the standard @xmath3 foamation functors .",
    "checking the relations for the 2-category @xmath156 needed to define foamation functors is a laborious task . here",
    "we utilize recent results of the first author with cautis showing that in a 2-representation with finitely many nonzero weight spaces many of the relations come for free  @xcite .",
    "an independent construction of the integral foamation functors into the usual @xmath3 foam @xmath1-category was given by mackaay , pan , and tubbenhauer in a recent update to their work in  @xcite .",
    "they utilize the foamation functors for a different application related to a generalization of khovanov s arc algebra to the @xmath3 setting .",
    "a careful analysis of cautis arguments in @xcite reveals that the skew howe duality approach also supplies a mechanism for equating different constructions of @xmath7 link homologies .",
    "indeed , given any 2-representation of @xmath145 whose objects are indexed by the nonzero weights in @xmath157 , and whose endomorphisms of the highest weight object are one dimensional in degree zero and zero dimensional otherwise , one obtains a unique knot homology theory that is formally determined by the relations imposed by the 2-representation . in section  [ sec_compare ]",
    ", we show that khovanov s @xmath4 and @xmath3 link homology theories fit into this framework .",
    "we also sketch a proof of the @xmath3 case of conjecture  @xmath158 from @xcite relating khovanov - rozansky link homology to the geometrically defined cautis - kamnitzer link homology , contingent on results to appear in @xcite .",
    "categorifying @xmath133 link invariants labeled by arbitrary ( non - fundamental ) representations appears to be a much more difficult problem  @xcite . in the @xmath9 case , there are several approaches to defining categorifications of the coloured jones polynomial by categorifying jones - wenzl projectors .",
    "the approach of cooper - krushkal uses foam based methods  @xcite , while another approach of frenkel , stroppel , and sussan uses lie theoretic methods  @xcite based on category @xmath159 for @xmath160 .",
    "these two approaches are compared and related via koszul duality in  @xcite .",
    "rozansky defined yet another approach to categorifying jones - wenzl projectors using complexes in bar - natan s foam category  @xcite .",
    "these complexes are presented as the stable limit of the complexes assigned to @xmath87-twist torus braids as @xmath161 , or `` infinite twists '' .",
    "this construction also agrees with the cooper - krushkal @xmath4 projectors .",
    "there are analogs of jones - wenzl projectors for @xmath133 . given a tensor product of fundamental @xmath20 representations ,",
    "there is a corresponding idempotent @xmath162 called a _ clasp _ following kuperberg s terminology from the @xmath3 case . for @xmath8",
    "these clasps were categorified by the third author using an @xmath3 foam based construction and a generalization of rozansky s infinite twist approach to projectors  @xcite .",
    "a related , but more general , approach using infinite twists was independently considered by cautis who showed that @xmath133 clasps can be categorified explicitly using the higher structure of categorified quantum groups  @xcite .",
    "his approach utilizes an infinite twist construction together with the categorified braid group action described above .",
    "given a reduced decomposition of @xmath163 of the longest braid word @xmath164 in the weyl group for @xmath165 , cautis defines a complex @xmath166 in @xmath167 .",
    "he shows that the infinite twist @xmath168 converges and categorifies the clasp @xmath169 in any appropriate @xmath1-representation .",
    "cautis categorified clasps are formulated explicitly using the 2-morphisms in @xmath145 .",
    "this is advantageous in that it allows for explicit computations not accessible within webster s formalism .",
    "given appropriate families of 2-representations of @xmath145 with nonzero weight spaces matching the vector space @xmath53 where @xmath51 and @xmath28 vary , cautis framework gives rise to @xmath133 knot homology theories and categorifications of @xmath133 clasps .",
    "cautis describes such 2-representations using derived categories of coherent sheaves . in section  [ sectionknothom ]",
    "we show that foamation functors allow cautis categorified clasps to be utilized in the foam setting . in the @xmath4 case",
    "this gives categorified projectors which can be viewed as an extension of the cooper - krushkal and rozansky projectors to the functorial foam categories of clark - morrison - walker and blanchet . in the @xmath3 case",
    "the resulting projectors agree with those from  @xcite .",
    "foams can be thought of as a categorification of webs .",
    "this perspective suggests that new insights into foam categories can be achieved through categorical skew howe duality . in  @xcite ,",
    "the authors use skew howe duality to deduce the @xmath133 web relations . in section  [ sec_deriving_rels ] , we show that this holds at the categorified level as well , namely that relations for @xmath4 and @xmath3 foams can be deduced from the categorified quantum group .",
    "this suggests that one may gain further insight to @xmath133 foams for @xmath170 using categorical skew howe duality . in a follow - up paper",
    ", we will give a foam - based construction of @xmath133 link homologies for @xmath170 which avoids the use of the kapustin - li formula @xcite .",
    "note that the relations we derive use graded parameters that are usually set to zero in the literature .",
    "these relations are similar to the ones of @xcite in the @xmath0 case , but in the @xmath171 case we obtain relations that slightly extend both blanchet s @xcite and clark - morrison - walker @xcite models .",

    "this work gives a categorification of ( a version of ) the category @xmath408 .",
    "we summarize this construction , which can be understood as a @xmath1-category defined as follows :    * objects are sequences of points in the interval @xmath409 $ ] , together with a zero object .",
    "* @xmath111-morphisms are formal direct sums of @xmath144-graded planar tangles with boundary corresponding to the sequences of points in the domain and codomain .",
    "* @xmath1-morphisms are formal matrices of @xmath173-linear combinations of degree - zero dotted cobordisms between such planar curves , modulo isotopy ( relative to the boundary ) and local relations .",
    "if we denote the @xmath144-grading of a planar tangle by the monomial @xmath410 for @xmath411 , then the degree of a cobordism @xmath412 is given by the formula @xmath413 where @xmath414 is the number of dots and @xmath415 is the number of boundary points in either @xmath416 or @xmath417 ( they agree ! ) .",

    "as mentioned in the introduction , the @xmath421 sign in the neck - cutting relation prevents us from defining a @xmath1-functor from @xmath403 to this @xmath1-category since it is incompatible with the sign in the nilhecke relation .",
    "we hence consider related versions of this construction .",
    "bar - natan formulates khovanov homology in the homotopy category of complexes in the above @xmath1-category , giving an invariant which is functorial only up to a @xmath422-sign under tangle cobordism .",
    "this functoriality issue was fixed by clark , morrison , and walker @xcite working in a related @xmath1-category of disoriented curves and cobordisms defined over the gaussian integers$ ] . ] ( see also the work of caprau @xcite , @xcite , @xcite for a related construction ) .",
    "blanchet @xcite later gave another functorial construction of khovanov homology in a related @xmath1-category defined over the integers .",
    "it turns out that in addition to fixing functoriality , these later constructions also fix the incompatibility of the neck - cutting and nilhecke relations .",
    "we will work in blanchet s enhanced foam model since it is more natural to consider from the perspective of skew howe duality and it avoids the introduction of complex coefficients .",
    "we return to the clark - morrison - walker ( cmw ) construction in the following section .",
    "we begin by defining a family of @xmath1-categories related to blanchet s construction which should be viewed as categorifications of the categories @xmath107 .",
    "@xmath423 is the @xmath1-category defined as follows :    * objects are sequences @xmath424 labeling points in the interval @xmath409 $ ] with @xmath425 and @xmath426 , together with a zero object . * @xmath111-morphisms are formal direct sums of @xmath144-graded enhanced @xmath171 webs - directed planar graphs with boundary with two types of edges - @xmath111-labeled edges @xmath427 \\draw[very thick , postaction={decorate } ] ( 0,-.5 ) -- ( 0,.5 ) ; \\end{tikzpicture } } ; \\endxy \\ ; \\ ; $ ] and @xmath1-labeled edges @xmath427 \\draw[double , postaction={decorate } ] ( 0,-.5 ) -- ( 0,.5 ) ; \\end{tikzpicture } } ; \\endxy \\ ; \\ ; $ ] - where all vertices are trivalent and take the following two forms : @xmath428 \\draw[double , postaction={decorate } ] ( 0,0 ) -- ( 0,1 ) ; \\draw[very thick , postaction={decorate } ] ( -.875,-.5 ) -- ( 0,0 ) ; \\draw[very thick , postaction={decorate } ] ( .875,-.5 ) -- ( 0,0 ) ; \\end{tikzpicture } } ; \\endxy \\qquad \\text { or } \\qquad \\xy ( 0,0 ) * { \\begin{tikzpicture } [ fill opacity=0.2 ,   decoration={markings ,                          mark = at position 0.6 with { \\arrow { > } } ;     } ] \\draw[double , postaction={decorate } ] ( 0,1 ) -- ( 0,0 ) ; \\draw[very thick , postaction={decorate } ] ( 0,0 ) -- ( .875,-.5 ) ; \\draw[very thick , postaction={decorate } ] ( 0,0 ) -- ( -.875,-.5 ) ; \\end{tikzpicture } } ; \\endxy \\quad .\\ ] ] @xmath111- ( respectively @xmath1- ) labeled edges are directed out from points labeled by @xmath111 ( respectively @xmath1 ) in the domain and directed into such labeled points in the codomain .",
    "no edges are attached to points labeled by @xmath95 . *",
    "@xmath1-morphisms are formal matrices of @xmath173-linear combinations of degree - zero @xmath4 foams - surfaces with oriented singular seams which locally look like the product of the letter @xmath429 with an interval - considered up to isotopy ( relative to the boundary ) and local relations .",
    "there are two types of facets of an @xmath171 foam , @xmath111-labeled and @xmath1-labeled , depending on which type of edge they are incident upon when the foam is expressed as a composition of elementary foams .",
    "the degree of a foam @xmath430 is given by the degree of the cobordism resulting from deleting all the @xmath1-labeled facets and edges and forgetting the orientation of the @xmath111-labeled edges .",
    "as in @xmath403 , we shall read diagrammatic depictions of webs and foams from right to left and from bottom to top . the orientation of a singular seam",
    "gives a cyclic ordering of the facets incident upon the seam via the right hand rule . by convention",
    ", a seam travels down through the first vertex in and up through the second ; this corresponds to the cyclic orientation of web vertices from @xcite .",
    "the relations for @xmath171 foams come from a non - local , universal construction detailed in @xcite ; however , we can exhibit a complete set of local relations giving an equivalent description of blanchet s work . in",
    "what follows , the @xmath1-labeled facets are depicted in yellow and @xmath111-labeled facets are drawn in red .",

    "the klr relations also fix the scaling on the composition of an @xmath554 and an @xmath555 crossing ; we choose to rescale the @xmath555 crossing .",
    "the scalings of the other @xmath1-morphisms again follow from the proof of theorem [ thm_cl ] .    at present time",

    "for this reason , we believe that @xmath423 is a more natural setting for the foamation @xmath1-functors ; in particular , we ll see in proposition [ prop_sl3_enhanced ] that the definition of the foamation functor from proposition [ prop_sl2 ] generalizes mutatis mutandis to give a foamation @xmath1-functor to an enhanced version of @xmath3 foams .      in this section",
    ", we recall the definition of the @xmath3 foam @xmath1-category and prove the existence of the @xmath3 foamation 2-functor .",
    "we then define an enhanced @xmath3 foam @xmath1-category similar to blanchet s @xmath4 foam category which appears naturally in the categorical skew howe context .",
    "finally , we give a functor from enhanced foams to standard foams , contrasting the @xmath4 case .      in @xcite",
    ", khovanov gives a foam based categorification of the @xmath3 link invariant .",
    "this construction was generalized by mackaay - vaz in @xcite and morrison - nieh in @xcite in the spirit of bar - natan s @xmath4 cobordism @xmath1-category @xcite , giving a categorification of kuperberg s @xmath3 spider @xcite .",
    "mackaay and vaz showed  @xcite that these foam based constructions of @xmath3 link homologies coincide with the @xmath8 case of khovanov and rozansky s @xmath133 link homologies defined via matrix factorizations  @xcite .",
    "we now recall the definition of this @xmath1-category , which we denote @xmath556 , using a hybrid of the above approaches :    * objects are sequences of points in the interval @xmath409 $ ] labeled by @xmath111 or @xmath1 , together with a zero object . * @xmath111-morphisms are formal direct sums of @xmath144-graded @xmath0 webs - directed , trivalent planar graphs with boundary in which each ( interior ) vertex is a sink or a source - where an edge is directed out from a point labeled by @xmath111 and into a point labeled by @xmath1 in the domain and vice - versa in the codomain . *",
    "@xmath1-morphisms are formal matrices of @xmath173-linear combinations of degree - zero @xmath3 foams - dotted surfaces with oriented singular seams which locally look like the product of the letter @xmath429 with an interval - considered up to isotopy ( relative to the boundary ) and local relations .    denoting the @xmath144-grading of a web by the monomial @xmath410 for @xmath411 , the degree of a foam @xmath557",

    "the direction of the singular seams keeps track of a cyclic ordering of the incident facets ; by convention , we take this ordering to be given by the right - hand rule .",
    "this convention is opposite to that used in @xcite and @xcite , hence one would expect to see opposite foam relations above ; however , we also reverse the relation between singular seams and trivalent vertices ( seams are directed up through source vertices and down through sink vertices ) which corresponds to taking different generating morphisms for the @xmath1-category .",
    "it is easy to see that the above @xmath1-category is isomorphic to the standard @xmath3 @xmath1-category .",
    "our conventions are chosen to align with those in the definition of the 2-category @xmath423 .",

    "we take inspiration from blanchet s @xmath171 foam construction in which the edges of webs labeled by @xmath1 and the corresponding facets of foams play a special role ( and in particular are not deleted ) .",
    "we hence define an @xmath0 foam @xmath1-category in which we retain @xmath116-labeled edges and the corresponding @xmath116-labeled facets .",
    "although such a construction is not suggested at the decategorified level ( as it was in the @xmath171 case ) we will see that the foamation functor is much more natural to define in this context and that an appropriately defined functor which forgets the @xmath116-labeled data gives a topological interpretation of the scalings .",

    "[ prop_sl3_enhanced ] the definition in proposition [ prop_sl2 ] describes a family of @xmath1-functors @xmath627 .    as before",
    ", we view the definition as showing the general image of each generating @xmath1-morphism ; edges connected to points labeled by @xmath95 and facets incident upon them are understood to be deleted .",
    "the proof of this proposition follows as in the proof of propositions [ prop_sl2 ] and [ prop_sl3 ] .",
    "the relations for the @xmath116-labeled facets allow us to delete any facet which does not meet the boundary ; however , this is not enough to define a forgetful functor @xmath628 .",
    "we can give such a rule by taking into account the boundary data .",
    "given a blanchet @xmath3 foam @xmath560 , define @xmath629 to be the euler characteristic of its @xmath116-labeled facets and let @xmath630 denote the number of @xmath116-labeled edges in the codomain of @xmath560 .",
    "let @xmath631 where @xmath632 is the @xmath0 foam obtained from @xmath560 by deleting the @xmath116-labeled facets ( and the @xmath116-labeled edges from the boundary webs ) .",
    "similarly , define @xmath633 to be the number of @xmath116-labeled edges in the domain of @xmath560 and @xmath634 and @xmath635 to be the number of points labeled by @xmath116 in the codomain and domain ( respectively ) of the webs between which @xmath560 maps ; of course , these later two denote the number of @xmath116-labeled vertical intervals on the left and right boundary of @xmath560 .",
    "[ sl3_forgetful ] the assignment @xmath636 defines a @xmath1-functor @xmath628 where objects are sent to themselves and enhanced webs are sent to the webs obtained by deleting the @xmath116-labeled edges .",

    "this construction is detailed in many places in the literature , in particular in @xcite , @xcite , and @xcite , so we will be brief . given a framed tangle @xmath739 with components labeled by irreducible representations , choose for each component a tensor product of fundamental representations having the corresponding irreducible as a highest weight subrepresentation . assign to the tangle the complex assigned to a cabling of the tangle ( we use here the fact that @xmath739 is framed ) with the categorified projector inserted along the cabling .",

    ".    one can show ( see @xcite , @xcite , or @xcite ) that the above invariant does nt depend on the choice of where the projector is inserted or which tensor product of fundamentals is used ( up to equivalence in the case that the tangle is not a link ) and gives a categorification of the reshetikhin - turaev invariant of framed tangles .",

    "his framework does not require the full structure of a 2-representation of @xmath145 , but rather the weaker data encoded in what he calls a categorical 2-representation .",
    "this weaker action is more like the data described in theorem  [ thm_cl ] without requiring the klr action .",
    "the klr relations greatly simplify the resulting complexes ; in particular , they imply analogs of the higher serre relation  @xcite and commutativity relations for divided powers  @xcite . using these relations , the complex @xmath808 associated to a link @xmath806",
    "can be reduced to a complex that only involves direct sums of the identity 1-morphism @xmath809 of @xmath810 , with various grading shifts .",
    "one does not actually need to know that the 2-representation @xmath334 categorifies @xmath805 ; it suffices that the nonzero weight spaces of @xmath805 parameterize the nonzero objects in @xmath334 .    applying the functor @xmath811 to the complex @xmath808 maps it to a complex of graded vector spaces .",
    "the number of @xmath809 summands and their grading shifts are formally determined by the categorified quantum group , hence so are the vector spaces appearing in the complex .",
    "the differentials depend only on the map @xmath812 , so it follows that this map completely determines the link homology theory .",
    "when the graded algebra @xmath813 is @xmath111-dimensional in degree zero and @xmath95 in all other degrees , only one such map exists , hence all constructions of @xmath133 link homology satisfying this condition are equivalent .",
    "after quotienting by the @xmath116-dotted sphere in the @xmath4 case and the @xmath116- , @xmath571- , and @xmath572-dotted spheres in the @xmath3 case , the foam @xmath1-categories satisfy this condition .",
    "this observation gives a method for showing that cautis - kamnitzer link homology is equivalent to khovanov - rozansky homology .",
    "using constructions from previous work  @xcite , cautis describes ( weak ) categorical 2-representations on derived categories @xmath814 of coherent sheaves on varieties arising as orbits in the affine grassmannian , as well as on coherent sheaves on nakajima quiver varieties @xmath815 .",
    "both of these categorical 2-representations are conjectured by cautis , kamnitzer , and licata to extend to 2-representations of @xmath145 . by the results of @xcite it suffices to prove",

    "the results from this paper will hence show that the foam based constructions of @xmath133 link homology agree with the cautis - kamnitzer construction for @xmath143 .",

    "in @xcite , cautis , kamnitzer , and morrison showed that the relations on @xmath7 webs could be derived via skew howe duality from the relations in @xmath54 .",
    "here we categorify this result in the @xmath143 case to show that many foam relations can be deduced from the assignments defining the foamation 2-functors @xmath773 and @xmath798 .",
    "the main result of this section is that all @xmath3 foam relations , all cmw @xmath4 foam relations ( assuming a strong form of locality ) , and many blanchet @xmath4 foam relations follow from relations in the categorified quantum group @xmath145 . in a follow - up paper",
    ", we study foam categories for arbitrary @xmath82 using this framework  @xcite .      since the blanchet foams arising as images under our @xmath1-functors must contain both @xmath111- and @xmath1-labeled facets ( unless they are identity foams ) and always bound webs whose edges are oriented leftward",
    ", we can not expect to recover all defining relations from the relations in @xmath156 .",
    "for example , we have no hope of recovering the @xmath111- and @xmath1-labeled neck - cutting relations or closed foam relations .",
    "there are nevertheless numerous foam relations arising from the quantum group relations , which we list below .",

    "<S> we show that khovanov homology ( and its @xmath0 variant ) can be understood in the context of higher representation theory . </S>",
    "<S> specifically , we show that the combinatorially defined foam constructions of these theories arise as a family of @xmath1-representations of categorified quantum @xmath2 via categorical skew howe duality . utilizing cautis - rozansky categorified clasps </S>",
    "<S> we also obtain a unified construction of foam - based categorifications of jones - wenzl projectors and their @xmath3 analogs purely from the higher representation theory of categorified quantum groups . in the @xmath4 case , this work reveals the importance of a modified class of foams introduced by christian blanchet which in turn suggest a similar modified version of the @xmath3 foam category introduced here . </S>"
